[30;1m198 | [0m[35m``compute_up``.  By default ``compute`` performs a ``bottom_up`` traversal.[0m
[30;1m199 | [0m[35mFirst it evaluates the leaves of the computation by swapping out keys for[0m
[30;1m200 | [0m[35mvalues in the input dictionary, ``{t: data}``.  It then calls ``compute_up``[0m
[30;1m201 | [0m[35mfunctions on these leaves to find intermediate nodes in the tree.  It repeats[0m
[30;1m202 | [0m[35mthis process, walking up the tree, and at each stage translating a Blaze[0m
[30;1m203 | [0m[35mexpression into the matching data element given the data elements of the[0m
[30;1m204 | [0m[35mexpression's children.  It continues this process until it reaches the root[0m
